store_data.merge(store_traffic, on='store_id', how='left')\nstore_data = store_data.merge(store_inv, on='store_id', how='left')\nstore_data = store_data.merge(store_promo_count, on='store_id', how='left')\nstore_data = store_data.merge(store_promo_discount, on='store_id', how='left')\nstore_data = store_data.merge(store_shelf, on='store_id', how='left')\nstore_data = store_data.merge(store_comp, on='store_id', how='left')\nstore_data = store_data.merge(store_visit_stats, on='store_id', how='left')\n\n# Fill missing\nfor col in store_data.select_dtypes(include=[np.number]).columns:\n    store_data[col] = store_data[col].fillna(0)\n\nprint(f\"Store data shape: {store_data.shape}\")\n\n# Step 1: Build a sales prediction model based on store characteristics\n# Features that reps cannot easily control: store_type, size, location, region, traffic, promotions\nfeature_cols = [\n    'store_size_sqm', 'avg_daily_traffic', 'promo_count', 'avg_discounted_price',\n    'total_ordered', 'avg_competitor_facings', 'competitor_promo_rate'\n]\n\n# Encode categorical variables\nle_store_type = LabelEncoder()\nle_location = LabelEncoder()\nle_region = LabelEncoder()\n\nstore_data['store_type_enc'] = le_store_type.fit_transform(store_data['store_type'])\nstore_data['location_enc'] = le_location.fit_transform(store_data['location'])\nstore_data['region_enc'] = le_region.fit_transform(store_data['region'])\n\ncategorical_features = ['store_type_enc', 'location_enc', 'region_enc']\nall_features = feature_cols + categorical_features\n\nX = store_data[all_features]\ny = store_data['total_revenue']\n\nprint(f\"Training sales prediction model...\")\nprint(f\"Features: {all_features}\")\nprint(f\"Samples: {len(X)}\")\n\n# Use GradientBoostingRegressor for prediction\nmodel = GradientBoostingRegressor(n_estimators=200, max_depth=5, min_samples_leaf=5, random_state=42)\nmodel.fit(X, y)\n\n# Get predictions and residuals\nstore_data['predicted_revenue'] = model.predict(X)\nstore_data['residual'] = store_data['total_revenue'] - store_data['predicted_revenue']\nstore_data['residual_pct'] = store_data['residual'] / store_data['predicted_revenue'] * 100\n\nprint(f\"Model R^2: {model.score(X, y):.4f}\")\n\n# Feature importance\nfi = pd.DataFrame({'feature': all_features, 'importance': model.feature_importances_})\nfi = fi.sort_values('importance', ascending=False)\nprint(\"Feature importance:\")\nprint(fi.to_string(index=False))\n\n# Step 2: For each rep, calculate performance metrics\n# First, determine which stores each rep is primary for\nstore_rep = visits.groupby(['store_id', 'rep_id']).size().reset_index(name='visit_count')\nstore_rep['rank'] = store_rep.groupby('store_id')['visit_count'].rank(ascending=False, method='dense')\n\n# Primary stores for each rep (rank == 1)\nprimary_stores = store_rep[store_rep['rank'] == 1][['rep_id', 'store_id']].copy()\n\n# Merge with store residuals\nprimary_perf = primary_stores.merge(\n    store_data[['store_id', 'total_revenue', 'predicted_revenue', 'residual', 'residual_pct',\n                'out_of_stock_rate', 'avg_facings', 'planogram_compliance_rate',\n                'endcap_rate', 'checkout_rate', 'promo_stand_rate', 'pos_materials_rate',\n                'avg_duration']],\n    on='store_id'\n)\n\n# Step 3: Aggregate by rep\n# For metrics that reps directly control (shelf quality, out-of-stock), look at ALL stores they visit\nrep_all_metrics = store_rep.merge(\n    store_data[['store_id', 'total_revenue', 'predicted_revenue', 'residual', 'residual_pct',\n                'out_of_stock_rate', 'avg_facings', 'planogram_compliance_rate',\n                'endcap_rate', 'checkout_rate', 'promo_stand_rate', 'pos_materials_rate',\n                'avg_duration', 'completion_rate', 'store_type', 'store_size_sqm', 'avg_daily_traffic']],\n    on='store_id'\n)\n\nrep_perf = rep_all_metrics.groupby('rep_id').agg(\n    # Store characteristics (for verification)\n    avg_store_size=('store_size_sqm', 'mean'),\n    avg_traffic=('avg_daily_traffic', 'mean'),\n    \n    # Sales performance across all stores\n    avg_residual=('residual', 'mean'),\n    avg_residual_pct=('residual_pct', 'mean'),\n    total_residual=('residual', 'sum'),\n    total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),\n    total_predicted=('predicted_revenue', 'sum'),\n    \n    # Controllable factors\n    avg_out_of_stock=('out_of_stock_rate', 'mean'),\n    avg_facings=('avg_facings', 'mean'),\n    planogram_compliance=('planogram_compliance_rate', 'mean'),\n    endcap_rate=('endcap_rate', 'mean'),\n    checkout_rate=('checkout_rate', 'mean'),\n    promo_stand_rate=('promo_stand_rate', 'mean'),\n    pos_materials_rate=('pos_materials_rate', 'mean'),\n    avg_duration=('avg_duration', 'mean'),\n    completion_rate=('completion_rate', 'mean'),\n    \n    # Weighted by visit count\n    weighted_residual=('residual', lambda x: np.average(x, weights=rep_all_metrics.loc[x.index, 'visit_count'])),\n).reset_index()\n\n# Also compute primary-only metrics\nprimary_perf_agg = primary_perf.groupby('rep_id').agg(\n    primary_avg_residual=('residual', 'mean'),\n    primary_avg_residual_pct=('residual_pct', 'mean'),\n    primary_total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),\n).reset_index()\n\nrep_perf = rep_perf.merge(primary_perf_agg, on='rep_id', how='left')\n\n# Step 4: Identify underperforming reps\n# Use residual_pct (percent difference from expected) as the main metric\n# A rep is underperforming if their stores consistently sell less than expected\n\nprint(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*80)\nprint(\"SALES REP PERFORMANCE ANALYSIS\")\nprint(\"=\"*80)\n\n# Sort reps by average residual (lowest first)\nrep_perf_sorted = rep_perf.sort_values('avg_residual_pct')\nprint(f\"\\nTop 10 worst performing reps (by avg residual %):\")\nprint(rep_perf_sorted[['rep_id', 'avg_residual_pct', 'avg_residual', 'primary_avg_residual_pct',\n                        'avg_out_of_stock', 'planogram_compliance', 'endcap_rate']].head(10).to_string(index=False))\n\nprint(f\"\\nTop 10 best performing reps (by avg residual %):\")\nprint(rep_perf_sorted[['rep_id', 'avg_residual_pct', 'avg_residual', 'primary_avg_residual_pct',\n                        'avg_out_of_stock', 'planogram_compliance', 'endcap_rate']].tail(10).to_string(index=False))\n\n# Statistical approach: identify outliers\nresiduals = rep_perf['avg_residual_pct'].values\nmean_res = np.mean(residuals)\nstd_res = np.std(residuals)\n\nprint(f\"\\nResidual distribution:\")\nprint(f\"Mean: {mean_res:.2f}%, Std: {std_res:.2f}%\")\nprint(f\"Min: {residuals.min():.2f}%, Max: {residuals.max():.2f}%\")\n\n# Z-score approach\nrep_perf['z_score'] = (rep_perf['avg_residual_pct'] - mean_res) / std_res\n\n# Also consider primary stores residual\nprimary_res = rep_perf['primary_avg_residual_pct'].values\nmean_primary = np.nanmean(primary_res)\nstd_primary = np.nanstd(primary_res)\nrep_perf['primary_z_score'] = (rep_perf['primary_avg_residual_pct'] - mean_primary) / std_primary\n\n# Combined score (negative = underperforming)\nrep_perf['combined_score'] = (rep_perf['z_score'] + rep_perf['primary_z_score'].fillna(rep_perf['z_score'])) / 2\n\nprint(f\"\\nReps with z_score < -1.5 (significantly underperforming):\")\nunderperform = rep_perf[rep_perf['combined_score'] < -1.5].sort_values('combined_score')\nprint(underperform[['rep_id', 'avg_residual_pct', 'z_score', 'primary_avg_residual_pct', 'combined_score',\n                     'avg_out_of_stock', 'planogram_compliance']].to_string(index=False))\n\nprint(f\"\\nReps with z_score < -1.0 (moderately underperforming):\")\nmod_under = rep_perf[rep_perf['combined_score'] < -1.0].sort_values('combined_score')\nprint(mod_under[['rep_id', 'avg_residual_pct', 'z_score', 'primary_avg_residual_pct', 'combined_score']].to_string(index=False))\n\n# Also check controllable factors for these underperformers\nprint(f\"\\nControllable factor comparison:\")\nprint(f\"{'Metric':<35} {'All Reps Avg':<15} {'Underperformers':<15}\")\nunderperform_ids = underperform['rep_id'].tolist()\nfor metric in ['avg_out_of_stock', 'avg_facings', 'planogram_compliance', 'endcap_rate', \n               'checkout_rate', 'promo_stand_rate', 'pos_materials_rate', 'avg_duration', 'completion_rate']:\n    all_mean = rep_perf[metric].mean()\n    under_mean = rep_perf[rep_perf['rep_id'].isin(underperform_ids)][metric].mean() if underperform_ids else 0\n    print(f\"{metric:<35} {all_mean:<15.4f} {under_mean:<15.4f}\")\n\n# Let's also do a more rigorous analysis: \n# For each rep, compute t-test comparing their primary stores' residuals to the population\nprint(f\"\\n\\nDetailed per-store analysis for all reps...\")\nstore_residuals = store_data[['store_id', 'residual', 'residual_pct', 'total_revenue', 'predicted_revenue']].copy()\n\n# Merge with primary rep\nstore_with_primary = store_residuals.merge(primary_stores, on='store_id')\n\n# For each rep, check if their primary stores are significantly worse\nrep_t_test_results = []\nfor rep_id in range(1, 101):\n    rep_stores = store_with_primary[store_with_primary['rep_id'] == rep_id]['residual_pct'].values\n    other_stores = store_with_primary[store_with_primary['rep_id'] != rep_id]['residual_pct'].values\n    \n    if len(rep_stores) > 0 and len(other_stores) > 0:\n        t_stat, p_val = stats.ttest_ind(rep_stores, other_stores, alternative='less')\n        rep_t_test_results.append({\n            'rep_id': rep_id,\n            't_stat': t_stat,\n            'p_value': p_val,\n            'mean_res_pct': np.mean(rep_stores),\n            'n_stores': len(rep_stores)\n        })\n\nrep_ttest = pd.DataFrame(rep_t_test_results)\nrep_ttest = rep_ttest.sort_values('p_value')\n\nprint(f\"\\nReps whose primary stores are significantly worse (p < 0.05, one-tailed):\")\nsig_under = rep_ttest[rep_ttest['p_value'] < 0.05]\nprint(sig_under[['rep_id', 'mean_res_pct', 't_stat', 'p_value', 'n_stores']].to_string(index=False))\n\n# Final determination: combine multiple signals\n# 1. Z-score of avg residual across all stores\n# 2. Z-score of avg residual across primary stores\n# 3. T-test p-value (primary stores vs others)\n# 4. Out-of-stock rate (higher is worse)\n# 5. Planogram compliance (lower is worse)\n\n# Create composite score\nrep_perf_final = rep_perf.merge(rep_ttest[['rep_id', 'p_value']], on='rep_id', how='left')\nrep_perf_final['p_value'] = rep_perf_final['p_value'].fillna(1.0)\n\n# Normalize and combine\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\n\nscaler = StandardScaler()\n# Negative signals: lower combined_score, lower planogram, higher out_of_stock\nscore_df = rep_perf_final[['combined_score', 'planogram_compliance', 'avg_out_of_stock', 'p_value']].copy()\nscore_df['neg_planogram'] = -score_df['planogram_compliance']\nscore_df['neg_p_value'] = -np.log10(score_df['p_value'].clip(lower=0.001))\n\n# Combine into a single underperformance score\n# Higher = more underperforming\nscore_cols = ['combined_score', 'neg_planogram', 'avg_out_of_stock', 'neg_p_value']\nfor c in score_cols:\n    score_df[c] = scaler.fit_transform(score_df[[c]]).flatten()\n\n# Invert combined_score so lower = worse\nscore_df['combined_score'] = -score_df['combined_score']\n\nrep_perf_final['underperformance_score'] = (\n    score_df['combined_score'] * 0.4 +\n    score_df['neg_planogram'] * 0.2 +\n    score_df['avg_out_of_stock'] * 0.2 +\n    score_df['neg_p_value'] * 0.2\n)\n\nprint(f\"\\n\\nFinal ranking (most underperforming first):\")\nfinal = rep_perf_final.sort_values('underperformance_score', ascending=False)\nprint(final[['rep_id', 'avg_residual_pct', 'primary_avg_residual_pct', 'combined_score',\n             'avg_out_of_stock', 'planogram_compliance', 'p_value', 'underperformance_score']].head(20).to_string(index=False))\n\n# Save results\nrep_perf_final.to_csv('/app/rep_analysis.csv', index=False)\nstore_data.to_csv('/app/store_analysis.csv', index=False)\n\nprint(\"\\n\\nAnalysis complete.
